When I opened the curtains, I found that I could see the port in the distance from the small corner of the window. When the weather was clear, I could see the sea through the dusty glass. The sea view room mentioned when booking was definitely not false advertising.
On the desk, there was a billboard saying that it was 699 yuan a night and also came with executive benefits and free afternoon tea. The small print indicated that it was not applicable from April 29 to May 2. Always remind you that you are the big loser who paid two or three times the price to stay during the May Day holiday. This feels greatüëç
There is no Chinese on the service phone. It is really an international hotel, but who made me not study hard when I was a child, and I am only half-level. I can only press 0 based on experience. After a long beep, someone finally answered the phone. This is the first time I call the service desk when I stay in a hotel, which makes me feel the feeling of waiting for the call to be connected. Others answer the phone after 2 or 3 beeps, which is too boring.
The room service staff was very enthusiastic. Seeing that our children had reminded us of the weather in Dalian, they gave us extra water and slippers. The service was very thoughtful. If I choose Nikko Hotel again next time, it must be because of that lady.
The staff in the buffet restaurant are more serious than those in other hotels. They will let the children compare their heights on the wall one by one. I like their work attitudeüëç
Zen Japanese Restaurant is delicious and inexpensive. The waiters are handsome and the women are beautiful. The environment is elegant. It is really a good place to eat, but don't order egg custard. If it is in the set meal, just give it up decisively, otherwise you will have to wait for a while. It is no exaggeration to say that the waiting time that day was enough to go back and forth to the Russian Style Street.
The parking lot is crowded, so you can go directly to B2.
Oh, by the way, this stay is absolutely worth it. The sound show was given as a gift. The first night was at eleven o'clock, and the midnight singing was heard. The rhythm was clear, and it felt like lying at the door of a KTV with poor sound insulation. At three thirty in the morning of the second night, I don't know if it was upstairs or next door, a battle between heaven and man, panting, howling, fierce and exciting! I heard this kind of sound show at Home Inn ten years ago.
This is the first time I wrote a review as a short essay. Hotel Nikko Dalian is great!

The most commendable thing is that the bathing equipment is excellent, and the toilet has heating and flushing functions. People who have higher requirements for hygiene will like it very much.
